Note that to produce these outputs, we used:
- tanh on the embeddings to compute the simulariry matrices
- relu activation function right before the last fc layer
- Adam optimizer
- the similarity measure is the cosine similarity
- we ignore sequences that contained more than half ["<unk>"]
- the black_list is simply ["<unk>"]
